# Scan Report: GSA.gov

- Issue: https://github.com/mgifford/open-scans/issues/1
- Submitted by: mgifford
- Scanned at: 2026-03-03T01:33:54.057Z
- Engines used: All engines (AXE, ALFA, Equal Access, AccessLint, QualWeb)
- Scan duration: 26.1 minutes
- Total URLs submitted: 100
- Accepted public URLs: 100
- Rejected URLs: 0
- 🌙 Dark mode: None of the scanned URLs support `prefers-color-scheme: dark`
- ALFA outcomes: 120581 passed, 8395 failed, 297 cantTell, 5487 inapplicable
- axe outcomes: 70782 passed, 327 failed, 227 cantTell, 5600 inapplicable
- Equal Access outcomes: 145104 passed, 1837 failed (1609 unique, 228 duplicate), 1588 cantTell, 0 inapplicable
- AccessLint outcomes: 8077 passed, 1123 failed (1123 unique, 0 duplicate), 0 cantTell, 0 inapplicable
- QualWeb outcomes: 50592 passed, 3339 failed, 13502 cantTell, 98 inapplicable
- Duplicate findings caught by later scanners: 10557

## 🔍 Cross-Page Patterns: Common HTML Issues

These HTML patterns cause the same accessibility errors across multiple pages. **Fix the pattern once in your codebase to fix it everywhere!**

### 🎯 Top Patterns to Fix (Highest Impact)

#### Pattern 1: Affects 67 page(s) - 67 occurrence(s)

**Scanner**: ALFA
**Rule**: [SIA-R111: Interactive elements have a sufficient target size](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r111)
**Issue**: Target has insufficient size

**HTML Pattern**:
```html
<a href="#" title="close" id="eb-close" class="eb-close pin-right pin-top z-top text-primary">...</a>
```

**XPath** (use in browser DevTools):
```
/a[@id="eb-close"]
```

**How to Replicate**:
1. Open any affected page in your browser
2. Press F12 to open DevTools
3. Go to Console tab
4. Run: `$x('/a[@id="eb-close"]')`
5. The element will be highlighted

**Affected Pages**:
- https://gsa.gov/about-us/find-apply-for-and-land-a-job-at-gsa
- https://gsa.gov/about-us/find-apply-for-and-land-a-job-at-gsa/discover-special-hiring-paths
- https://gsa.gov/about-us/find-apply-for-and-land-a-job-at-gsa/elevate-your-professional-career
- https://gsa.gov/about-us/find-apply-for-and-land-a-job-at-gsa/get-an-internship
- https://gsa.gov/about-us/find-apply-for-and-land-a-job-at-gsa/launch-your-career
- *...and 62 more page(s)*

## Detailed Failure Information (ALFA)

### https://gsa.gov/about-us/find-apply-for-and-land-a-job-at-gsa

#### Rule: [SIA-R111: Interactive elements have a sufficient target size](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r111)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<a href="#" title="close" id="eb-close" class="eb-close pin-right pin-top z-top text-primary">...</a>`
- XPath: `/a[@id="eb-close"]`

**Failure 2:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<button class="tbm-link level-1 no-link tbm-toggle" tabindex="0" aria-expanded="false" type="button">...</button>`
- XPath: `/button[@class="tbm-link level-1 no-link tbm-toggle"]`

**Failure 3:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<button class="tbm-link level-1 no-link tbm-toggle active-trail" tabindex="0" aria-expanded="false" type="button">...</button>`
- XPath: `/button[@class="tbm-link level-1 no-link tbm-toggle active-trail"]`

**Failure 4:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<a title="Per diem lookup" class="usa-nav__menu-item" id="perdiem-link" data-scroll-to="perdiem-section" href="javascript:;" data-fancybox="" data-src="#lookup-dialog">           Per diem lookup         </a>`
- XPath: `/a[@id="perdiem-link"]`

**Failure 5:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<a class="print-page usa-tooltip__trigger" onclick="window.print()" href="javascript:;" id="print_page" data-position="top" aria-describedby="tooltip-996560" tabindex="0">...</a>`
- XPath: `/a[@id="print_page"]`

*... and 10 more failures for this rule*

#### Rule: [SIA-R3: lang attribute has a valid language code](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r3)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The element does not have a unique ID
- HTML: `<div class="usa-card__img usa-fixed padding-x-0" id="undefined">...</div>`
- XPath: `/div[@id="undefined"]`

**Failure 2:**
- Message: The element does not have a unique ID
- HTML: `<img src="https://www.gsa.gov/system/files/Careers-01-internship-1200x800.jpg" imagesize="undefined" is_downloadable="undefined" id="undefined" alt="Five young people in conference at a table covered with books and laptops, in front of a wall of books on shelves" class=" img-responsive" />`
- XPath: `/img[@id="undefined"]`

#### Rule: [SIA-R56: Landmarks with the same role are distinguishable](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r56)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: Some `search` have the same name.

#### Rule: [SIA-R57: Landmarks don't repeat the same content](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r57)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The text is not included in a landmark region

#### Rule: [SIA-R66: Text has enhanced contrast with its background](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r66)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The highest possible contrast of the text is 5.9:1 which is         below the required contrast of 7:1

### https://gsa.gov/about-us/find-apply-for-and-land-a-job-at-gsa/get-an-internship

#### Rule: [SIA-R111: Interactive elements have a sufficient target size](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r111)

- XPath: `/img[@id="img_166641_0_0_113"]`

**Failure 3:**

- XPath: `/a[@id="perdiem-link"]`

## Detailed Failure Information (axe)

### https://gsa.gov/about-us/find-apply-for-and-land-a-job-at-gsa

#### Rule: [region](https://dequeuniversity.com/rules/axe/4.11/region?application=playwright)
**Impact**: moderate

**Failure 1:**
- Message: All page content should be contained by landmarks

**Failure 1:**

- XPath: `.current`

**Failure 3:**
- Message: ARIA attributes must conform to valid names
- HTML: `<a class="paginate_button " aria-controls="child-care-centers-table" aria-role="link" data-dt-idx="1" tabindex="0">2</a>`
- XPath: `a[data-dt-idx="1"]`

**Failure 4:**
- Message: ARIA attributes must conform to valid names

#### Rule: [aria-valid-attr](https://dequeuniversity.com/rules/axe/4.11/aria-valid-attr?application=playwright)
**Impact**: critical

**Failure 1:**
- Message: ARIA attributes must conform to valid names
- HTML: `<a class="paginate_button previous disabled" aria-controls="hb-listings" aria-disabled="true" aria-role="link" data-dt-idx="previous" tabindex="-1" id="hb-listings_previous">Previous</a>`
- XPath: `#hb-listings_previous`

**Failure 2:**
- Message: ARIA attributes must conform to valid names
- HTML: `<a class="paginate_button current" aria-controls="hb-listings" aria-role="link" aria-current="page" data-dt-idx="0" tabindex="0">1</a>`
- XPath: `.current`

**Failure 3:**
- Message: ARIA attributes must conform to valid names
- HTML: `<a class="paginate_button " aria-controls="hb-listings" aria-role="link" data-dt-idx="1" tabindex="0">2</a>`
- XPath: `a[data-dt-idx="1"]`

**Failure 4:**
- Message: ARIA attributes must conform to valid names
- HTML: `<a class="paginate_button " aria-controls="hb-listings" aria-role="link" data-dt-idx="2" tabindex="0">3</a>`
- XPath: `a[data-dt-idx="2"]`

**Failure 5:**
- Message: ARIA attributes must conform to valid names
- HTML: `<a class="paginate_button " aria-controls="hb-listings" aria-role="link" data-dt-idx="3" tabindex="0">4</a>`
- XPath: `a[data-dt-idx="3"]`
